তীব্র এসিড ও মৃদু ক্ষার - মিথাইল অরেঞ্জ, মিথাইল রেড;<br>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: সালোকসংশ্লেষণে বেগুনি-নীল ও কমলা-লাল আলো বেশি ব্যবহৃত হয়। একক আলো হিসেবে লাল আলোতে সালোকসংশ্লেষণ বেশি হয়।<br>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: NaOH এ পরমাণু = 3টি;<br>
∴ 1 mol NaOH এ পরমাণু সংখ্যা = <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-57-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>(</mo><mn>6.02</mn><mo>&amp;#xD7;</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>23</mn></mrow></msup><mo>&amp;#xD7;</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1.8</mn><mo>&amp;#xD7;</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>24</mn></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-507" style="width: 12.83em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 10.494em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.027em, 1010.49em, 2.379em, -999.998em); top: -2.006em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-508"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-509" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">(</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-510" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">6.02</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-511" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">×</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-512" style="padding-left: 0.207em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.764em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.24em, 1000.95em, 4.182em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-513" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">10</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.424em; left: 0.986em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-514"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-515"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-516" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">23</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-517" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">×</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-518" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">3</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-519" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-520" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-521" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">1.8</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-522" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">×</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-523" style="padding-left: 0.207em;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.764em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.24em, 1000.95em, 4.182em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-524" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">10</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.424em; left: 0.986em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-525"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-526"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-527" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">24</span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.01em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.348em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.453em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>6.02</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>23</mn></mrow></msup><mo>×</mo><mn>3</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>1.8</mn><mo>×</mo><msup><mn>10</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>24</mn></mrow></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-57">\rm (6.02×10^{23}×3) =1.8×10^{24}</script></span> টি।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৪০০]</p>
